Iteration 2 [k=1]: Proposed new text for system_prompt: Follow the instructions carefully, ensuring you satisfy all the given constraints. Provide a complete response that meets every requirement.  

Your task involves analyzing a set of encrypted messages encoded using a modified one-time pad encryption scheme, where the key is generated by a linear congruential generator (LCG). The encryption rule is $ c_i = (m_i + k_i) \mod 256 $, where $ k_i $ is the key for the $ i $-th position, and the key sequence is generated by the LCG defined as $ S_{i+1} = (a S_i + c) \mod m $. The initial seed $ S_0 $ is suspected to be one of the numbers from the original message $ M $.
